5:24pm&lt;/abbr&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  &lt;a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Public" class="uiStreamPrivacy inlineBlock fbStreamPrivacy fbPrivacyAudienceIndicator _5pcq" href="#" role="button"&gt;&lt;i class="lock img sp_VTao_RYfyVB sx_44fe27"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a4a624286269e21022558" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;LGBTQ Deportation = Death&lt;br /&gt;  Please help by donating! If you cannot donate please share this post to others who might be able to help. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Sulma was born and raised in Guatemala City, Guatemala. Six years ago, she began her journey to the United States and away from her abusive stepfather. While it was difficult to leave her family, she knew that survival for her meant leaving her home country and seeking refuge elsewhere because her work as an LGBTQ activist had put her in danger&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt;. In 2009 Sulma  fled to Texas, was detained by ICE and sent to the Hutto detention center in Taylor, TX.  Four months later Sulma had proven credible fear and was released from Hutto as an asylee. At this point Sulma had a renewable work permit contingent on her visits to ICE offices once every three months that was until one day on June 25, 2014 when she was detained once again during a routine check in with ICE. She was then sent to Eloy Detention Center in Arizona where she spent 8 horrific months. The officials there questioned her sexuality and then separated her because of her LGBTQ identity. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class="text_exposed_show"&gt;&lt;p&gt; Thanks to the community pressure and a $15,000 bond Sulma was released back to her family in Austin, Texas-\-\- but the nightmare is not over as ICE has an order for her deportation. Sulma sought sanctuary  on June 11th, 2015 and has been at the First Unitarian Universalist Church in Austin since then fighting to stay home. We need your help to keep Sulma home, any amount of money you donate will help with the many associated expenses. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;a data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a4a6242979f6b59949185" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;Over the last 25 years the reputation of Mao Zedong has been seriously undermined by ever more extreme estimates of the numbers of deaths he was supposedly responsible for. In his lifetime, Mao Zedong was hugely respected for the way that his socialist policies improved the welfare of the Chinese people, slashing the level of poverty and hunger in China and providing free health care and education. Maos theories also gave great inspiration to those fighting imperialism aroun&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt;d the world. It is probably this factor that explains a great deal of the hostility towards him from the Right. This is a tendency that is likely to grow more acute with the apparent growth in strength of Maoist movements in India and Nepal in recent years, as well as the continuing influence of Maoist movements in other parts of the world.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class="text_exposed_show"&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;a  &lt;span&gt;&lt;a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Show edit history" class="uiLinkSubtle" ajaxify="/ajax/edits/browser/post/?content_token=829037167182439" rel="dialog" href="#" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;+E&quot;&#125;" role="button"&gt;Edited&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  &lt;a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Public" class="uiStreamPrivacy inlineBlock fbStreamPrivacy fbPrivacyAudienceIndicator _5pcq" href="#" role="button"&gt;&lt;i class="lock img sp_VTao_RYfyVB sx_44fe27"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a4a6242a48a1318924772" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;Lal Salam Comrade Behrooz Navaii, Who was assisting us on formulating some programs that we will one day launch in his revolutionary memory! Here are the words from our Comrades in Los Angeles who worked closely with Comrade Behrooz who lives on in our hearts and in our struggle! Long live Behrooz Long live MLM &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;br /&gt; &quot;It&#039;s with a heavy heart that we hear that comrade Behrooz Navaii has passed away, and so we inform the rest of comrades online of his passing. His brother informed &lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt;most of us recently after we noticed that he was missing from radical circles in Los Angeles for more than a week.&lt;br /&gt; Behrooz was a former member of Peoples Fadaee Guerrillas of Iran and had to flee Iran after the situation was heavily comrpomised. He eventually came to the United States and went to school in the Bay Area. It was there that he continued his communist organizing. And years later, after moving to Los Angeles, we are proud to say that he was among our comrades in the Red Guards - Los Angeles as a regular participant in our events, our movie screenings, our study groups and our international solidarity work, especially with the Maoist Communist Party of Manipur.&lt;br /&gt; Whenever a comrade falls, we have to continue that necessary work of building for a proletarian revolution. Behrooz was consistent in urging us to be more militant, to grow, to continue to get mass support, to continue to organize oppressed nationalities.&lt;br /&gt; So, Behrooz, we&#039;re sorry that you&#039;re gone. We will miss you.&lt;br /&gt; Lal Salaam!&quot;- RGLA&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt; &lt;span class="text_exposed_link"&gt;&lt;a class="see_more_link" onclick="var func = Angeles, specifically in Boyle Heights and East Los Angeles. Since our formation on October 4, 2014, weve been affiliated with the New Communist Party (Liaison Committee) (NCP-LC) as part of the organizations mission to forge a new Maoist communist party in the alt="&#039;Solidarity with Comrade Ajith! 
 68-year-old revolutionary Maoist veteran Murali Kannampilly, better known to the international communist struggle as Comrade Ajith was arrested this month on May 8th 2015 by the anti-terrorism squad of Maharashtra.  Comrade Ajith was captured during a follow-up visit to a hospital while recovering from recent heart surgery.  At the hospital he was accused of presenting false documents, as well as membership in the Communist Party of India (Maoist) or CPI-Maoist, the foremost revolutionary party which has been banned by the Indian state and operates underground. 
  Comrade Ajith is well known among communists in the USA for his polemic titled &#x201c;Against Avakianism&#x201d; in which he masterfully attacks and exposes the revisionism and cultish degeneration of the revolutionary communist party USA and their leader Bob Avakian. 
 In an elegant clarification of MLM, he states, 
 &#x201c;There is continuity from Marx, to Lenin, to Mao (and that includes the contributions of Engels and Stalin).  But the understanding of this ideology was not the same in each stage. The party concept of Marx&#x2019;s, Lenin&#x2019;s and Mao&#x2019;s times were not the same.  In fact, to speak of a Leninist party without imbibing the advance achieved by Mao, including his correction of some of the aberrations that had crept in would be going backward. This is why we must today speak of the Maoist party. Today the key link is Maoism, not Leninism, not just on the party but on all aspects of communist theory and practice.  This can be recognized by those who firmly grasp Maoism&#x201d;
 Our comrade, considered by the reactionary Indian state to be &#x201c;one of Keralas most wanted Maoists,&#x201d; is said by friends and comrades to be a soft spoken, dedicated revolutionary, who put the interests of the people above himself.  Authorities have alleged that Ajith is responsible for organizing hundreds of cadres in Kerala. The son of the Indian Diplomat to China, and a former engineering student, Cde. Ajith has spent the last four decades living underground, traveling and organizing, his mobility attributed to the fact that very few photographs exist of him.  He has also been arrested before in connection with an attack on the Kayanna police station by the Maoists in 1976.  At that time arbitrary arrests were common and intellectuals as well as civil rights activists and armed rebels were picked up and held for an indeterminate amount of time and without trial.
  Comrade Ajith was released after more than a year and went underground, becoming a full time organizer with CPI-ML. Since the mid 70&#x2019;s he has been associated with the ongoing Maoist revolution in India (sometimes referred to as the Naxal movement)  and various groups espousing Maoist ideology, he has written five books and stands as one of the people&#x2019;s war&#x2019;s ideological leaders.  Comrade Ajith is a committed Maoist fighter who has dedicated his life to the revolution and to the oppressed.  As a leader of CPI-Maoist he was the only member to represent India at the Revolutionary International Movement conference in 1984.
  We extend solidarity and revolutionary love to Comrade Ajith and all those who continue to fight for the liberation and restructuring of India, to the CPI-Maoist, Indian people and Comrade Ajith we say: Lal Salam! (red salute!) &#x2013; Red Guard.&#039;" width="199" height="110" /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href="/redguardsaustin/photos/pb.722986724454151.-2207520000.1436853794./812603685492454/?type=1" rel="theater" ajaxify="/redguardsaustin/photos/pb.722986724454151.-2207520000.1436853794./812603685492454/?type=1&amp;src=https%3A%2F%2Fscontent-lax1-1.xx.fbcdn.net%2Fhphotos-xpa1%2Ft31.0-8%2F11133911_812603685492454_7361261745599448431_o.jpg&amp;smallsrc=https%3A%2F%2Fscontent-lax1-1.xx.fbcdn.net%2Fhphotos-xpa1%2Fv%2Ft1.0-9%2F10428435_812603685492454_7361261745599448431_n.jpg%3Foh%3Ddaa3cdb49b782db80b87ad82e913b9f9%26oe%3D5653BD15&amp;size=1280%2C698&amp;fbid=812603685492454&amp;source=29&amp;player_origin=pages"&gt;&lt;div class="uiScaledImageContainer _5v4k" style="width:110px;height:110px;"&gt;&lt;img class="scaledImageFitHeight img" src="https://scontent-lax1-1.xx.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xpa1/v/t1.0-9/s206x206/10428435_812603685492454_7361261745599448431_n.jpg?oh=6c41623260312327355c54d6014b114a&amp;oe=5612FB50" style="left:-58px;" alt="&#039;STATEMENT OF SOLIDARITY WITH THE WOMEN OF AUSTIN&#039;S EAST SIDE. 

Reactionary.

     adjective - &quot;of, pertaining to, marked by, or favoring reaction, especially extreme conservatism or rightism in politics; opposing political or social change .&quot;

1.     Red Guards Austin stands with women. We defend their right to choose and their right to safe abortion. We seek to help create a society where safe, healthy abortions are provided upon request- free of charge. We stand in solidarity with the women of our community, who are principally women of color. Solidarity means a commitment to defending our rights to safe abortion and serving the people against white male reactionaries who seek to control women, restrict their choices, or intimidate them into submission. Our principle is that those who uphold such backwardness should be prevented from harming the community and isolated accordingly.
 
2.     Alex Jones of infowars.com has taken it upon himself to blame Red Guards Austin for the fiasco that resulted from his effort to co-opt and infiltrate the Black Lives Matter movement by organizing a demonstration against a Planned Parenthood location that serves mostly working class women of color. In essence, Alex Jones has tried to take the blame off the police who murder Black people every 28 hours, and instead place it on working class Black women.  This did not work out so well when people from the community disrupted and shut down his attempt. If he blames us, let us then own it and say that it is right to rebel against reactionaries! We seek to turn the old world upside down, smash it to pieces and make a big mess. The bigger the mess, the better. We are committed to our community and we are not afraid to stand and fight as was proven when six pro-women activists went against 50 reactionary &#x201c;infowarriors&#x201d; and succeeded in their task without arrest. 

3.     Black Lives Matter. We stand in unwavering solidarity with the rebellions in Ferguson, Baltimore and others inspired by the BLM movement. We hold the police and the reactionary apologists for the pig system accountable for the loss of Black Lives. We show solidarity to the People&#039;s Task Force and other organizers who have put time and effort into this movement in Austin and we do not accept or tolerate the co-opting of this movement for an anti-choice agenda. We know that this system is not broken; that it works this way by design and we demand justice for the victims of the police, including Larry Jackson, Freddie Gray, Sophia King and all other Black lives taken by the police. We seek to defend this movement against all those who would trivialize it or turn it around to blame the victims of this unjust and disgusting capitalist system. 

4.     Capitalism forces the majority of oppressed nations to live in poverty, and in a situation of institutional violence that prevents women from being able to afford raising children. This is a violence condoned and enforced daily by this exploitative system. These same right wing fascist scum who follow Alex Jones oppose all socialized health care, all standardized living, food stamps and anything else poor working people rely on to survive, in favor of rampant privatization. Their position is not &#x201c;pro-life&#x201d;, it is anti-women and anti-working class. They have no interest in the survival of Black children, but are quick to try and remove women&#x2019;s choice regarding their own bodies. 

5.     Alex Jones seeks to make pro-choice activists home addresses public for his wingnut fascist supporters to access. He encourages violence against women activists by compromising their safety and exposing them to his unstable and violent supporters. We are ready for the reality of this situation and have taken every precaution to defend both ourselves and our community from any threat whatsoever and, in the words of Malcolm X, &#x201c;by any means necessary.&quot; We also have resources and anyone interested in protesting or visiting Alex Jones should have fair access to his addresses which we will provide upon request, all of his houses including the one in West Lake, the one in Dripping Springs and the one in the Amli building penthouse high rise down town.  We know as much about their circles as they could ever hope to know about ours. We will be posting updates of photos, names, addresses and license plates of known racists who associate with infowars and the conspiracy theorist crowd in general. 

6.     Our main task however is not to fight pathetic attempts at fake activism. We aim to build revolution and take workers control. We have no fear and will continue resolutely in our work. 

&#x201c;It is good if we are attacked by the enemy, since it proves that we have drawn a clear line of demarcation between the enemy and ourselves. It is still better if the enemy attacks us wildly and paints us as utterly black and without a single virtue; it demonstrates that we have not only drawn a clear line of demarcation between the enemy and ourselves but achieved a great deal in our work.&#x201d; -Mao Tse-tung

&#x201c;To die for the people is weightier than Mount Tai, but to work for the fascists and die for the exploiters and oppressors is lighter than a feather.&#x201d; &#x2013; Mao Tse-tung&#039;" width="203" height="110" /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href="/redguardsaustin/photos/pb.722986724454151.-2207520000.1436853794./811668728919283/?type=1" rel="theater" ajaxify="/redguardsaustin/photos/pb.722986724454151.-2207520000.1436853794./811668728919283/?type=1&amp;src=https%3A%2F%2Fscontent-lax1-1.xx.fbcdn.net%2Fhphotos-xpt1%2Ft31.0-8%2F11313137_811668728919283_8520457200973375321_o.jpg&amp;smallsrc=https%3A%2F%2Fscontent-lax1-1.xx.fbcdn.net%2Fhphotos-xfa1%2Fv%2Ft1.0-9%2F10929942_811668728919283_8520457200973375321_n.jpg%3Foh%3D1eab142498bf371fc38e3ea272a0e544%26oe%3D56228288&amp;size=924%2C1158&amp;fbid=811668728919283&amp;source=29&amp;player_origin=pages"&gt;&lt;div class="uiScaledImageContainer _5v4k" style="width:110px;height:110px;"&gt;&lt;img class="scaledImageFitWidth img" src="https://scontent-lax1-1.xx.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xfa1/v/t1.0-9/p110x80/10929942_811668728919283_8520457200973375321_n.jpg?oh=c1191d3613f5e0794dcb067513b3debe&amp;oe=56220B64" alt="&#039;Happy Birthday and Revolutionary salute to Yuri Kochiyama!

 &lt;a class="" rel="dialog" ajaxify="/ajax/timeline/sign_up_dialog/?page_id=722986724454151&amp;next=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fredguardsaustin%2Fposts%2F427871917415375" href="https://www.facebook.com/r.php?fbpage_id=722986724454151&amp;r=111"&gt;Share&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class="uiUfi UFIContainer" id="u_ps_0_1_8"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/form&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li class="_5kjq" id="u_ps_0_1_6"&gt;&lt;div class="_4-u2 _4-u8"&gt;&lt;div class="_4-u3 _5kjo"&gt;&lt;div class="clearfix"&gt;&lt;span class="_5kjs lfloat _ohe"&gt;&lt;img class="_s0 img" src="https://fbcdn-profile-a.akamaihd.net/hprofile-ak-xta1/v/t1.0-1/c0.7.40.40/p40x40/11752172_10207160640395955_9208772459852981558_n.jpg?oh=7bc815bdb43cfa159e58db5be53c8709&amp;oe=56237B21&amp;__gda__=1445073429_2df9ed152e63b97def5c93aaed9268c2" alt="" style="width:40px;height:40px" /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="_50f3 _50f7"&gt;Morgan Le Fay Hughes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a class="_5kjp uiLinkSubtle" href="/redguardsaustin/posts/10207101293712325"&gt;&lt;abbr title="Sunday, July 5, 2015 at 2:05pm" data-utime="1436130320"&gt;July 5 at 2:05pm&lt;/abbr&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Public" class="uiStreamPrivacy inlineBlock fbStreamPrivacy fbPrivacyAudienceIndicator" href="#" role="button"&gt;&lt;i class="lock img sp_VTao_RYfyVB sx_44fe27"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="_50f3"&gt;&lt;i class="mrs img sp_RSqc-PyJQym sx_e29fad"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a4a6228dba01254278814" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;a class="_58cn" href="/hashtag/convergeagainsttheklan?source=feed_text&amp;story_id=10207101293712325" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;*N&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:104&#125;"&gt;&lt;span aria-label="hashtag" class="_58cl"&gt;#&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="_58cm"&gt;ConvergeAgainstTheKlan&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;! On Saturday, July 18th, the Loyal White &lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt;Knights of the Ku Klux Klan will assemble on the statehouse grounds in Columbia, SC. And we will confront them.
This rally is part of a recent wave of anti-Black terror, from the Charleston massacre to the arson of Black churches, that has strategically sought to build upon a white racist backlash against the &lt;a class="_58cn" href="/hashtag/blacklivesmatter?source=feed_text&amp;story_id=10207101293712325" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;*N&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:104&#125;"&gt;&lt;span aria-label="hashtag" class="_58cl"&gt;#&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="_58cm"&gt;BlackLivesMatter&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, anti-police uprisings of the past year.
We call upon all those who can&#x2014;#BlackLivesMatter activists, community organizers, anti-racists, anarchists and other radicals, and anyone else furious with racism and the police&#x2014;to converge on Columbia, confront the Klan, and defy their message of white supremacy. History has shown&#x2014;from the armed standoff against a lynch mob in Columbia, TN, in 1946 to the 1958 Battle of Hayes Pond, from the Deacons for Defense to the armed defiance of Monroe, NC&#x2019;s NAACP chapter, from the 1979 Greensboro Massacre to the 1997 confrontation with the Klan in downtown Asheville, NC&#x2014;that we must oppose white supremacist organizing actively and physically, in our streets and neighborhoods.
The KKK is only a small group, whose ability to inflict racist violence actually pales in comparison to that of structures of oppression like the police, the economy, and the state. But the sentiment that groups like the KKK hold runs deep through the currents of whiteness in this country, and is a major obstacle to our struggles against these larger structures. Explicit manifestations of white supremacy like the Klan are one way that the state will seek to contain the #BlackLivesMatter organizing and anti-police riots of the last year; at this historic juncture, a large Klan rally in the South cannot go unchallenged.
Bring banners, bring a friend, and bring your anger and rage against the white supremacy that courses through the veins of this society. See you in Columbia. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt; &lt;span class="text_exposed_link"&gt;&lt;a class="see_more_link" onclick="var func = function(e) &#123; e.preventDefault();
